Here's a step-by-step guide to finding an internship in the tech industry:
Figure out and explore the field of tech: Start by gaining a broad understanding of the different areas within the tech industry. Research various domains such as software development, data science, cybersecurity, artificial intelligence, web development, and more. This will help you get a sense of the available opportunities and the skills required in each field.
Identify your passions: Once you have a basic understanding of different tech domains, reflect on your interests and strengths. Consider the projects or subjects that excite you the most. It could be building websites, analyzing data, creating mobile applications, or any other area that aligns with your skills and interests. Identifying your passions will guide you towards internships that resonate with your goals.
Research companies and internship programs: Look for companies or organizations that offer internships in your chosen tech domain. Explore their websites, careers pages, and job portals to find relevant internship openings. Pay attention to the skills they require and the projects they work on. Researching the companies will give you an idea of their culture, values, and the opportunities they provide.
Find 10 good projects to contribute to: Once you have identified potential internship opportunities, start exploring open-source projects, community initiatives, or company projects that align with your interests. Look for projects where you can make meaningful contributions and gain hands-on experience. This could involve working on GitHub repositories, contributing to open-source software, or collaborating on side projects. Aim to find at least 10 projects that you can actively participate in.
Engage with the tech community: Actively participate in the tech community by attending meetups, conferences, or online forums related to your interests. Engaging with professionals and like-minded individuals will expand your network and provide valuable insights. Contribute to discussions, ask questions, and seek guidance from experienced individuals in your desired tech domain. Building relationships within the community can lead to internship opportunities or valuable referrals.
Showcase your work on Twitter and in the community: Establish an online presence by creating a professional Twitter account or leveraging other social media platforms. Share your projects, achievements, and learnings with the community. Engage in conversations, follow industry influencers, and participate in relevant hashtags. Additionally, showcase your work through a personal portfolio website or a GitHub profile. This will help you build credibility and visibility among potential employers.
By following these steps, you can navigate the process of finding an internship in the tech industry. Remember to stay proactive, continuously learn and improve your skills, and leverage your network to increase your chances of securing a rewarding internship opportunity.

5/28/23, 9:23 AM - Siddharth: @919427122421 @918000397375 tell me quality

1-month Social Media Content Plan for Cocoden on LinkedIn

Objective: To increase engagement and generate leads on LinkedIn for Cocoden, an AI-powered office suite.

Target Audience: 
1. Small business owners and entrepreneurs 
2. Remote workers 
3. Professionals looking for productivity tools 

Social Media Platform: LinkedIn 

5-3-2 Rule: 
- 5 pieces of curated content 
- 3 pieces of original content 
- 2 pieces of personal content 

Week 1:
- Curated content: Share articles from Forbes, Inc. and Entrepreneur Magazine about productivity, remote work and AI technology.
- Original content: Share a blog post about how Cocoden has helped remote workers to be more productive. Create a video demonstrating the features of Cocoden.
- Personal content: Share a photo of Cocoden team enjoying a productive day at work.

Week 2:
- Curated content: Share articles discussing the benefits of AI in the workplace and how it can decrease workload. 
- Original content: Share a blog post on how small business owners can use Cocoden to be more efficient in their daily tasks.
- Personal content: Share a photo of the team's workspace and the Cocoden software being used in action.

Week 3:
- Curated content: Share industry insights and news related to AI and productivity.
- Original content: Share a case study demonstrating the ROI for businesses that have implemented Cocoden. 
- Personal content: Share a photo of the team's weekly meeting discussing productivity goals.

Week 4:
- Curated content: Share articles discussing the future of AI in the workplace.
- Original content: Share a blog post about the benefits of using Cocoden in sales and marketing operations.
- Personal content: Share a photo of team members using Cocoden in different ways to improve their workflow.

Overall, the focus is on sharing high-quality content that provides value to our audience while also showcasing the benefits of Cocoden. By consistently sharing a mix of curated, original and personal content, we aim to engage our target audience and generate leads for our AI-powered office suite.
5/28/23, 9:40 AM - Siddharth: @917567048512 Brand story for DashVsSleep

Once upon a time, there was a truck driver named Jack. Jack loved his job, but he often found himself driving through the night for long hours, trying to make his deliveries on time. 

One night, while driving through a particularly dark and lonely stretch of road, Jack began to feel drowsy. He tried everything he could think of to stay awake - slapping himself, blasting the radio, even rolling down the window and letting the cold night air whip across his face. But no matter what he did, he couldn't shake the feeling of exhaustion that was creeping over him. 

Just when it seemed like Jack was about to drift off to sleep, he heard a loud and insistent alarm coming from his dashboard. Startled, he sat up straight and looked around, trying to figure out what was going on. Then he saw it - a small device that he had installed on his dashboard, called DashVsSleep. 

The device had been monitoring Jack's driving behavior all along, and when it noticed the telltale signs of drowsiness - slow reaction times, erratic swerving, and so on - it had sounded the alarm, jolting him back to wakefulness. 

From that moment on, Jack knew that he had found his hero's tool - the one thing that would keep him safe and alert on even the longest, darkest nights. And he wasn't alone - other drivers soon began to hear about DashVsSleep, and they too realized that it was the key to staying alert and focused on the road. 

Thanks to DashVsSleep, truck drivers everywhere can now rest easy knowing that they have a powerful ally on their side, keeping them safe and sound as they navigate the highways and byways of the world. The journey may be long and winding, but with DashVsSleep, they're always in good hands.
5/28/23, 9:42 AM - Siddharth: @918000397375 @919427122421 Brand Story for Cocoden

Once upon a time, there was a world where office productivity was a constant struggle. Employees had to use multiple tools and platforms to manage their tasks, and communication between teams was often disjointed and inefficient. That was until Cocoden arrived - the ultimate AI-powered office tool suite designed to revolutionize the way we work.

Our story begins with the call to adventure- the realization that there is a need for a better way to manage office tasks. Cocoden is the answer - it empowers teams to streamline their workflow and collaborate seamlessly, enabling them to focus on what really matters - their core competencies. With features like AI-powered chatbots and personalized task management, Cocoden helps teams work together with clarity and efficiency.

As with every good story, there are challenges to overcome. In this case, it's breaking through the noise in the crowded market of office productivity tools. The journey is not without setbacks and obstacles, but Cocoden perseveres because it is grounded in the belief that it can truly make a difference in the way people work.

With guidance from advisors and experts, Cocoden refines its approach and hones in on its unique value proposition. Through rigorous testing and continuous improvement, the product emerges as a true game-changer in the industry.

Finally, Cocoden emerges victorious, with teams all over the world adopting it as their go-to office productivity tool suite. It becomes a trusted ally to those who use it every day and a beacon of hope for those still struggling with outdated and inefficient processes. Cocoden's hero's journey has come full circle, and it stands ready to assist others on their own journeys towards success.

In summary, Cocoden's brand story is one of transformation and triumph against the odds. It's a story about innovation and progress in a world that's always evolving. At its heart, Cocoden is about empowering teams to achieve their best work - and that's a journey worth taking.

6/21/23, 9:40 AM - Siddharth: Wrote small write-up on quantization:

All quantization stuff is based on one thing at bottom -  very small percentage of weights can create performance issue when we compress them, here they used "non-uniform quantization" where buckets for quantization are not uniform while compression. 

So, sensitive weights can be kept in higher precision. 

Also, weights are stored in dense form but where full precision is needed, they are sparse. 

Paper name: SqueezeLLM, 230% speedup.

1. India is low trust society, difficult to make people pay upfront (FMCG me pure year ka subscription hota hai)

    download_images(dest, urls=results[:200])
    resize_image(dest, max_size=400, dest=dest)

10/8/23, 11:22 AM - Siddharth: Via GPT:

Brainstorm Seed Keywords: Start by making a list of seed keywords related to your app's content. These should be broad terms related to gardening, plants, and home gardening. For example:

"Gardening tips"
"Indoor plants"
"Plant care"
"Plant encyclopedia"
"Home gardening guide"
Use Keyword Research Tools: Utilize keyword research tools like Google Keyword Planner, SEMrush, or Ahrefs to expand your list of keywords. These tools can provide insights into search volume, competition, and related keywords.

Analyze Competitor Keywords: Look at competitors or similar apps in the gardening and plant care niche. Identify keywords they are targeting successfully. You can use tools like SEMrush or SpyFu for competitor analysis.

Long-Tail Keywords: Target long-tail keywords (phrases with more than three words) that are specific to the topics covered in your app. For instance:

"How to care for snake plant indoors"
"Best fertilizer for tomato plants"
"Identifying common houseplant pests"
Consider User Intent: Think about the intent behind specific keywords. Are users looking for information, tips, products, or services? Tailor your content accordingly.

Local SEO: If your app provides information on regional gardening or local plant varieties, consider targeting location-based keywords. For example:

"Gardening tips for [Your City]"
"Local plant nurseries in [Your State]"
Content Optimization: Once you've identified target keywords, optimize your app's content, including blog posts and plant profiles, with these keywords. Ensure that your content is high-quality, informative, and relevant to the keywords you're targeting.

Monitor and Update: SEO is an ongoing process. Continuously monitor your keyword rankings, user engagement, and the performance of your content. Update and improve your content regularly to stay competitive and meet user needs.

Link Building: Consider building high-quality backlinks to your app from reputable gardening websites, blogs, and forums. This can improve your app's authority and search engine rankings.

User Experience: Don't forget the importance of a smooth user experience on your app. Page load speed, mobile optimization, and user-friendly navigation all contribute to SEO success.
